  4947:   function aicmMajorItemStatusLabelR8O(row) {
  4948:     var handoff = String(row && row.handoff_status_code || "");

  4954:     if (decomposition === "done" || decomposition === "completed") return "分解済";
  4955:     return "未実行";
  4956:   }
